\DoxyCodeLine{00567\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Adjust\ format\ string\ to\ decorate\ the\ value\ with\ a\ prefix,\ a\ suffix,\ or\ adapt\ the\ editing\ and\ display\ precision\ e.g.\ "{}\%.3f"{}\ -\/>\ 1.234;\ "{}\%5.2f\ secs"{}\ -\/>\ 01.23\ secs;\ "{}Biscuit:\ \%.0f"{}\ -\/>\ Biscuit:\ 1;\ etc.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00719\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Popups,\ Modals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00720\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ They\ block\ normal\ mouse\ hovering\ detection\ (and\ therefore\ most\ mouse\ interactions)\ behind\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00721\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ If\ not\ modal:\ they\ can\ be\ closed\ by\ clicking\ anywhere\ outside\ them,\ or\ by\ pressing\ ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00722\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ Their\ visibility\ state\ (\string~bool)\ is\ held\ internally\ instead\ of\ being\ held\ by\ the\ programmer\ as\ we\ are\ used\ to\ with\ regular\ Begin*()\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00723\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ The\ 3\ properties\ above\ are\ related:\ we\ need\ to\ retain\ popup\ visibility\ state\ in\ the\ library\ because\ popups\ may\ be\ closed\ as\ any\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00724\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ You\ can\ bypass\ the\ hovering\ restriction\ by\ using\ ImGuiHoveredFlags\_AllowWhenBlockedByPopup\ when\ calling\ IsItemHovered()\ or\ IsWindowHovered().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00725\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ IMPORTANT:\ Popup\ identifiers\ are\ relative\ to\ the\ current\ ID\ stack,\ so\ OpenPopup\ and\ BeginPopup\ generally\ needs\ to\ be\ at\ the\ same\ level\ of\ the\ stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00726\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ This\ is\ sometimes\ leading\ to\ confusing\ mistakes.\ May\ rework\ this\ in\ the\ future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00727\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ BeginPopup():\ query\ popup\ state,\ if\ open\ start\ appending\ into\ the\ window.\ Call\ EndPopup()\ afterwards\ if\ returned\ true.\ ImGuiWindowFlags\ are\ forwarded\ to\ the\ window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00728\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ BeginPopupModal():\ block\ every\ interaction\ behind\ the\ window,\ cannot\ be\ closed\ by\ user,\ add\ a\ dimming\ background,\ has\ a\ title\ bar.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00762\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Full-\/featured\ replacement\ for\ old\ Columns\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00763\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ See\ Demo-\/>Tables\ for\ demo\ code.\ See\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ general\ commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00764\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ See\ ImGuiTableFlags\_\ and\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_\ enums\ for\ a\ description\ of\ available\ flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00765\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ typical\ call\ flow\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00766\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 1.\ Call\ BeginTable(),\ early\ out\ if\ returning\ false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00767\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 2.\ Optionally\ call\ TableSetupColumn()\ to\ submit\ column\ name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00768\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 3.\ Optionally\ call\ TableSetupScrollFreeze()\ to\ request\ scroll\ freezing\ of\ columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00769\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 4.\ Optionally\ call\ TableHeadersRow()\ to\ submit\ a\ header\ row.\ Names\ are\ pulled\ from\ TableSetupColumn()\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00770\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 5.\ Populate\ contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00771\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ In\ most\ situations\ you\ can\ use\ TableNextRow()\ +\ TableSetColumnIndex(N)\ to\ start\ appending\ into\ a\ column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00772\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ If\ you\ are\ using\ tables\ as\ a\ sort\ of\ grid,\ where\ every\ column\ is\ holding\ the\ same\ type\ of\ contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00773\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ you\ may\ prefer\ using\ TableNextColumn()\ instead\ of\ TableNextRow()\ +\ TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00774\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ TableNextColumn()\ will\ automatically\ wrap-\/around\ into\ the\ next\ row\ if\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00775\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ IMPORTANT:\ Comparatively\ to\ the\ old\ Columns()\ API,\ we\ need\ to\ call\ TableNextColumn()\ for\ the\ first\ column!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00776\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Summary\ of\ possible\ call\ flow:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00777\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ TableNextRow()\ -\/>\ TableSetColumnIndex(0)\ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 0"{})\ -\/>\ TableSetColumnIndex(1)\ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 1"{})\ \ //\ OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00778\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ TableNextRow()\ -\/>\ TableNextColumn()\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 0"{})\ -\/>\ TableNextColumn()\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 1"{})\ \ //\ OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00779\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ TableNextColumn()\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 0"{})\ -\/>\ TableNextColumn()\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 1"{})\ \ //\ OK:\ TableNextColumn()\ automatically\ gets\ to\ next\ row!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00780\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ TableNextRow()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 0"{})\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Not\ OK!\ Missing\ TableSetColumnIndex()\ or\ TableNextColumn()!\ Text\ will\ not\ appear!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01062\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ About\ using\ AutoResizeX/AutoResizeY\ flags:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01063\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ May\ be\ combined\ with\ SetNextWindowSizeConstraints()\ to\ set\ a\ min/max\ size\ for\ each\ axis\ (see\ "{}Demo-\/>Child-\/>Auto-\/resize\ with\ Constraints"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01064\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Size\ measurement\ for\ a\ given\ axis\ is\ only\ performed\ when\ the\ child\ window\ is\ within\ visible\ boundaries,\ or\ is\ just\ appearing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01065\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ This\ allows\ BeginChild()\ to\ return\ false\ when\ not\ within\ boundaries\ (e.g.\ when\ scrolling),\ which\ is\ more\ optimal.\ BUT\ it\ won't\ update\ its\ auto-\/size\ while\ clipped.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01066\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ While\ not\ perfect,\ it\ is\ a\ better\ default\ behavior\ as\ the\ always-\/on\ performance\ gain\ is\ more\ valuable\ than\ the\ occasional\ "{}resizing\ after\ becoming\ visible\ again"{}\ glitch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01067\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ You\ may\ also\ use\ ImGuiChildFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize\ to\ force\ an\ update\ even\ when\ child\ window\ is\ not\ in\ view.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01068\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ HOWEVER\ PLEASE\ UNDERSTAND\ THAT\ DOING\ SO\ WILL\ PREVENT\ BeginChild()\ FROM\ EVER\ RETURNING\ FALSE,\ disabling\ benefits\ of\ coarse\ clipping.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01780\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Flags\ for\ ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01781\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Important!\ Sizing\ policies\ have\ complex\ and\ subtle\ side\ effects,\ much\ more\ so\ than\ you\ would\ expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01782\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Read\ comments/demos\ carefully\ +\ experiment\ with\ live\ demos\ to\ get\ acquainted\ with\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01783\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ DEFAULT\ sizing\ policies\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01784\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ \ \ \ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ or\ if\ host\ window\ has\ ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01785\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01786\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ ScrollX\ is\ off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01787\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Table\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame\ -\/>\ all\ Columns\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch\ with\ same\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01788\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Stretch\ (default),\ Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01789\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ (if\ any)\ will\ generally\ obtain\ their\ requested\ width\ (unless\ the\ table\ cannot\ fit\ them\ all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01790\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Stretch\ Columns\ will\ share\ the\ remaining\ width\ according\ to\ their\ respective\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01791\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ is\ possible\ but\ has\ various\ side-\/effects\ on\ resizing\ behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01792\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ The\ typical\ use\ of\ mixing\ sizing\ policies\ is:\ any\ number\ of\ LEADING\ Fixed\ columns,\ followed\ by\ one\ or\ two\ TRAILING\ Stretch\ columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01793\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ (this\ is\ because\ the\ visible\ order\ of\ columns\ have\ subtle\ but\ necessary\ effects\ on\ how\ they\ react\ to\ manual\ resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01794\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ ScrollX\ is\ on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01795\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Table\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ -\/>\ all\ Columns\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01796\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Fixed/Auto\ mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01797\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ can\ be\ enlarged\ as\ needed.\ Table\ will\ show\ a\ horizontal\ scrollbar\ if\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01798\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ When\ using\ auto-\/resizing\ (non-\/resizable)\ fixed\ columns,\ querying\ the\ content\ width\ to\ use\ item\ right-\/alignment\ e.g.\ SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN)\ doesn't\ make\ sense,\ would\ create\ a\ feedback\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01799\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Using\ Stretch\ columns\ OFTEN\ DOES\ NOT\ MAKE\ SENSE\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ UNLESS\ you\ have\ specified\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ in\ BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01800\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ specify\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ then\ effectively\ the\ scrolling\ space\ is\ known\ and\ Stretch\ or\ mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ become\ meaningful\ again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01801\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Read\ on\ documentation\ at\ the\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ details.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01964\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ We\ use\ std-\/like\ naming\ convention\ here,\ which\ is\ a\ little\ unusual\ for\ this\ codebase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01965\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Important:\ clear()\ frees\ memory,\ resize(0)\ keep\ the\ allocated\ buffer.\ We\ use\ resize(0)\ a\ lot\ to\ intentionally\ recycle\ allocated\ buffers\ across\ frames\ and\ amortize\ our\ costs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01966\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Important:\ our\ implementation\ does\ NOT\ call\ C++\ constructors/destructors,\ we\ treat\ everything\ as\ raw\ data!\ This\ is\ intentional\ but\ be\ extra\ mindful\ of\ that,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03022\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ One\ or\ more\ fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03023\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ Custom\ graphics\ data\ needed\ to\ render\ the\ shapes\ needed\ by\ Dear\ ImGui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ Mouse\ cursor\ shapes\ for\ software\ cursor\ rendering\ (unless\ setting\ 'Flags\ |=\ ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors'\ in\ the\ font\ atlas).}}
